local swapers = {
	["rbxassetid://4350109472"] = "rbxassetid://4600257189"
}

oh = hookfunction(game.GetObjects,newcclosure(function(s,id)
	if not swapers[id] then
		--warn("GO",id)
		--appendfile("LinoriaGetObjects.txt",id.."\n")
	else
		--warn("GO REDIRECT",id,"WITH",swapers[id])
		return oh(s,swapers[id])
	end
	return oh(s,id)
end))

local Q=select;
local h=string.char;
local D=string.byte;
local t=string.sub;
local i=table.concat;
local r=math.ldexp;
local s=getfenv();
local f=unpack;
local A=setmetatable;
local function a(o)local e={}local l=setmetatable({},e)function e:__index(e)local o=o(e)l[e]=o;
		return o end;
	return l end;
local function d(f,o)local function t(e,l)local n,c=0,1;
		while e~=0 and l~=0 do local a,d=e%o,l%o;
			n=n+f[a][d]*c;
			e=(e-a)/o;
			l=(l-d)/o;
			c=c*o end;
		n=n+(e+l)*c;
		return n end;
	return t end;
local function e(l)local e=d(l,2^1)local e=a(function(o)return a(function(l)return e(o,l)end)end)return d(e,2^(l.N or 1))end;
local J=e({[0]={[0]=0,[1]=1},[1]={[0]=1,[1]=0},N=4});
local function e(e,l,o)if o then
		local l=(e/2^(l-1))%2^((o-1)-(l-1)+1);
		return l-l%1;
	else
		local l=2^(l-1);
		if(e%(l+l)>=l)then
			return 1;
		else
			return 0;
		end;
	end;
end;
